Subject: Apache only starts correctly in single process mode when trying to run a dso version of the server.
X-Send-Pr-Version: 3.110

>Synopsis:       Apache only starts correctly in single process mode when trying to run a dso version of the server.

>Environment:

OSF1 V5.1 732 alpha
>Description:
I am writing a dso module for apache on Tru64 V5.1. Apache without my module works find. It works perfectly in single process mode ( httpd -X ) as well. I can request pages without a problem. However, when I attempt to run the server as it is meant to be run (apachctrl start ), no child process are created - at least child processes that execute the child_main function. Unfortunately there is no core dump, nor an error written to the error log.

With the alpha-trace program I have traced execution of my server. The trace shows that a few child processes try and execute either the program cat, or kill.

I have pasted the entirety of this file below:

>How-To-Repeat:
I suppose it would be rather hard to repeat. But the details of my compilation are below:

The dso molue I am building links to the following libraries:
gcc -v -fPIC -shared -Wl,-B,symbolic -o ./debug/libct_apache_plugin.so \
debug/ct_request_data_impl.o debug/ct_log_impl.o debug/ct_apache_mod.o debug/ct_server_funcs_impl.o debug/ct_server_parms_impl.o debug/ct_web_server_config_impl.o debug/certutil.o debug/coca.o debug/cocacook.o debug/cocathrd.o debug/ct_format_output.o debug/ct_global.o debug/ct_multi_auth.o debug/ct_plugin_server.o debug/ct_request_data.o debug/ct_server_proxy.o debug/form-lib.o debug/hitsd.o debug/ct_init.o debug/ct_log.o debug/ct_message.o debug/ct_request.o debug/ct_auth_server_pool.o debug/ct_auth_server_pool_utils.o debug/ct_error.o debug/ct_web_server_config.o debug/ct_update_key_thread.o debug/ct_multi_auth_unix.o -lm -lrt -lc   -lpthread   -L../../../common/mux/./debug -lmux  -L../../../common/mem/./debug -lmem  -L../../../common/sfl/./debug -lsfl  -L../../../common/net/./debug -lctnet  -L../../../common/fope/./debug -lfope  -L../../../common/util/./debug -lct_util  -L../../../common/coca/./debug -lcoca  -L../../../common/alpha-Tru64/./debug -losutil  -L../../../../libraries/alpha-Tru64/openssl/ -lssl  -L../../../../libraries/alpha-Tru64/openssl -lcrypto    -L../../../../libraries/alpha-Tru64/apache_1.3/ -lhttpd   

We do have a call to dlopen for extensions of this module.

The apache server was compiled with the following options:
    ./configure --prefix=/path/to/apache --enable-module=most --enable-shared=max --enable-rule=SHARED_CORE

I also added -lpthread to the /src/Makefile LIBS1 variable.
>Fix:
At this point I do not have a way of fixing this problem. I have seen one other reference on the web to a similar problem, and their solution was to run the statically linked version of the server.

Any help or insight would be greatly appreciated.
